# <a name="release-notes-for-office-current-channel-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-103">Office 的发布笔记当前频道（预览）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-103">Release Notes for Office Current Channel (Preview)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-104">本文包含 Windows 桌面版的 Word、Excel、PowerPoint、Outlook、Access、Project 和 Teams 的当前频道（预览）内部版本的发行说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-104">This article contains release notes for Current Channel (Preview) builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, Project, and Teams for Windows desktop.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-105">每周，我们都会提供精彩集锦，其中包含我们希望你了解的有趣新功能、重要修补程序和所有重要问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-105">Every week, we’ll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-106">请注意，我们经常会过一段时间就将功能（有时甚至是修补程序）发布到当前频道（预览）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-106">Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Current Channel (Preview) over a period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-107">这可以让我们确保将功能向更多的受众发布之前，所用功能均可正常使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-107">This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-108">因此，如果你没有看到下面所述的功能，请不要担心，你最终会获取这些功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-108">So, if you don’t see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span></span>  


> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-109">发行说明发布日期可能与实际内部版本发布日期不一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-109">The release notes publication date may not match the actual build release date.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-110">Microsoft Teams 的功能可能不同于最新发布的当前频道预览版，因为前者具有更高的发布频率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-110">Microsoft Teams features may differ from the latest Current Channel Preview released as they have a more frequent release cadence.</span></span>

## <a name="version-2106-june-25"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-113">版本 2106：6 月 25 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-113">Version 2106: June 25</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-114">*版本 2106（内部版本 14131.20250）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-114">*Version 2106 (Build 14131.20250)*</span></span>

[//]: # (请勿移除错误详细信息内容开头)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-116">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-116">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-117">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-117">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-118">我们修复了导致对某些用户禁用翻译选项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-118">We fixed an issue that caused the translation options to be disabled for some users.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-119">遇到过此 bug 的客户在导航到“文件”->“选项”->“语言”时，将会看到其翻译选项已禁用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-119">Customers who experienced this bug would have seen their translation options disabled when navigating to File -> Options -> Language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-120">正因如此，客户将无法更改其首选翻译语言和其他翻译相关设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-120">Due to this, they would have been unable to change their preferred translation language and other translation related settings.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-121">我们修复了导致拥有很多共享日历的“共享的日历改进项”选项用户遇到一些性能问题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-121">We fixed an issue that caused users of the Shared Calendar Improvements option who have many shared calendars to experience some performance issues.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-122">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-122">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-123">我们修复了由于 PowerPoint 特定对话框受到阻碍、用户无法在“Windows 安全”对话框中输入凭据以打开文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-123">We fixed an issue where a user was unable to enter credentials into a Windows Security dialog to open a file, because of an obstructive PowerPoint-specific dialog.</span></span>


### <a name="visio"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-124">Visio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-124">Visio</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-125">拥有来宾访问权限的 SPO/ODB 链接现在将适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-125">SPO/ODB Links with guest access will now work.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-126">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-126">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-127">修复了在受密码保护的 docx 文件上持续引用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-127">Fixed an issue to persist citations on a password protected docx file.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-133">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-133">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-134">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-134">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-135">**心无旁骛地阅读邮件：** 通过打开沉浸式阅读器，更轻松地专注于具有自定义文本间距、页面颜色、列宽和线条焦点的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-135">**Read messages with fewer distractions:** Make it easier to focus on messages with custom text spacing, page colors, column width, and line focus by turning on Immersive Reader.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-136">**上次登录/可疑登录：** Outlook 现在会告诉你上次登录帐户的登录时间和位置，如果检测到任何可疑登录活动，将会发出警报</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-136">**Last Sign In / Suspicious Sign In:** Outlook now tells you when and where you last signed into your account, and alerts you if any suspicious sign-in activity is detected</span></span>

## <a name="version-2106-june-07"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-150">版本 2106：6 月 7 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-150">Version 2106: June 07</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-153">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-153">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-154">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-154">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-155">修复了阻止名称管理器打开包含大量隐藏名称的书籍的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-155">We fixed an issue that prevented the Name Manager from opening books with a large number of hidden names.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-156">修复了填充大量数据时影响 VLOOKUP 和 INDEX/MATCH 性能的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-156">We fixed an issue that impacted the performance of VLOOKUP and INDEX/MATCH when filling a large amount of data.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-157">修复了在 RealTimeData 函数引用时导致动态数组不更新单元格值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-157">We fixed an issue that caused Dynamic Arrays to not update cell values when referenced by RealTimeData functions.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-158">修复了输入法的改写模式未在字符上键入，而是将它们留在字符串末尾这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-158">Fixed an issue where IME's OverType mode was not typing over characters, it left them at the end of the string.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-159">修复了使用冻结窗格时与两指滚动有关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-159">We fixed an issue related to two-finger scrolling when using freeze panes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-160">修复了在大型打印机上打印时与内存不足相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-160">We fixed an issue related to out of memory issues when printing on large-format printers.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-161">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-161">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-162">我们修复了在仅下载标题模式下运行时，导致用户看到可操作邮件不断刷新，或者在下载后还原到标题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-162">We fixed an issue that caused users to see actionable messages either constantly refreshing or reverting back to headers after download when running in Download Headers Only mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-163">我们修复了用户无法在“非商业”许可 Outlook 版本中的文件夹间移动项目这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-163">We fixed an issue where users were unable to move items across folders in "non-business" licensed Outlook versions.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-164">我们修复了从存档存储中删除文件夹时导致用户意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-164">We fixed an issue that caused users to experience a unexpected close when removing folders from an archive store.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-165">我们修复了在加载人员卡片时导致某些用户遭遇意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-165">We fixed an issue that caused some users to experience a unexpected close when loading person cards.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-166">我们修复了一个问题，对于拥有永久许可证的用户，该问题导致 Outlook 中的人员选取器向上扩展，而不是向下扩展。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-166">We fixed an issue that caused the people picker in Outlook to expand upwards rather than downwards for users with a perpetual license.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-167">我们修复了导致 Office Perpetual 2021 预览版用户无法显示反馈选项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-167">We fixed an issue that caused the feedback option to fail to appear for users of the Office Perpetual 2021 preview.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-168">我们修复了导致用户看不到其“发件箱”文件夹中所有已发送邮件的副本这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-168">We fixed an issue that caused users to see copies of all of their sent items appearing in their Outbox folder.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-169">我们修复了一个问题，该问题导致自定义域的用户在将链接粘贴到电子邮件时看到关于权限的警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-169">We fixed an issue that caused users of custom domains to see a warning message about permissions when pasting a link into an email message.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-170">我们添加了一个注册表项，该注册表项禁用了新的会议室查找工具体验（与 Outlook for Web 中相同的体验），并启用旧版会议室查找工具和"建议时间"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-170">We added a registry key that disables the new Room Finder experience (the same experience as in Outlook for Web) and enables the legacy Room Finder with Suggested Times.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-171">注册表项:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-171">Registry Key:</span></span>

    ><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-172">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Options\Calendar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-172">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Options\Calendar</span></span> </br>
    > <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-173">REG_DWORD “ShowLegacyRoomFinder”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-173">REG_DWORD “ShowLegacyRoomFinder”</span></span></br></br>
    > <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-174">0(默认) - 当用户点击‘会议室查找器’按钮搜索可用会议室时，Outlook 会使用新的会议室查找器 OWA 支持的体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-174">0 (default) - Outlook uses new Room Finder OWA Powered eXperience when user clicks 'Room Finder' button to search for available rooms</span></span>  </br>
    > <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-175">1 - Outlook 使用旧版会议室查找工具 UI 搜索可用会议室</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-175">1 - Outlook uses legacy Room Finder UI to search for available rooms</span></span> </br>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-176">我们修复了将大声朗读与其他版本的 Windows 一起使用时导致意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-176">We fixed an issue that caused an expected close when using read aloud with other versions of Windows.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-177">我们修复了从存档存储中删除文件夹时导致用户遭遇挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-177">We fixed an issue that caused users to experience a hang when removing folders from an archive store.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-178">我们修复了在加载人员卡片时导致某些用户遭遇崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-178">We fixed an issue that caused some users to experience a crash when loading person cards.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-179">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-179">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-180">修复了只读模式下时阻止从演讲者备注窗格进行复制的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-180">We fixed an issue that prevented copying from the speaker notes pane while in Read Only mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-181">我们修复了一个问题，以确保将使用栏上的“重试保存”按钮保存的文件添加到“最近列表”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-181">We fixed an issue to ensure that a file saved using the Retry Save button on the bus bar is added to the Recent List.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-182">修复了少数用户无法使用重用幻灯片选项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-182">Fixed an issue where Reuse Slides option was not available for few users.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-183">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-183">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-184">修复了手动计划任务中的分配移动到错误日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-184">We fixed an issue where assignments on manually scheduled tasks could be moved to an incorrect date.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-185">修复了资源池无响应且无法打开的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-185">We fixed an issue where the resource pool was unresponsive and couldn't be opened.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-186">修复了创建自定义字段公式时，使用特定日期或时间参数的 ProjectDate */ProjectDur* 函数生成错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-186">We fixed an issue where an error was generated if you created a custom field formula that used the ProjectDate */ProjectDur* functions with specific date or time parameters.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-187">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-187">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-188">修复了发布后批注暂时为空白的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-188">Fixes an issue where a  comment is temporarily blank after posting.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-189">修复了用户选择放弃更改之后仍然显示“另存为”错误消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-189">We fixed an issue where a Save As error message was displayed even after a user chose to discard changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-190">修复了阻止将图像发布在新式批注中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-190">We fixed an issue that prevented images from being posted in modern comments.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-191">我们修复了按组合键（如 Ctrl + shift + @）无法生成预期的重音符号（本例中为“å”）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-191">We fixed an issue where pressing key combinations such as ctrl + shift + @ would not produce the expected accented character( in this case, 'å').</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-192">我们解决了与图像压缩相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-192">We fixed an issue related to image compression.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-193">我们修复了审阅窗格可以滚动或似乎可以滚动，但与所选批注不对齐这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-193">We fixed an issue where the Reviewing pane could scroll or appear to scroll but didn't align with selected comment.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-194">修复了将文档导出为 PDF 时未保存某些批注的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-194">We fixed an issue where some comments were not saved when exporting a document to PDF.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-195">修复了应用“受限编辑”时，未受保护文档区域阻止编辑新批注的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-195">We fixed an issue that prevented the editing of a new comment in an unprotected area of a document when Restricted Editing is applied.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-196">修复了不需要滚动动画相关问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-196">We fixed an issue related to unneeded scrolling animation.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-197">修复了批注窗格意外关闭这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-197">Fixed an issue where the comments pane closed unexpectedly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-198">我们修复了选择批注时未突出显示批注这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-198">We fixed an issue where comments aren't highlighted when selected.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-199">我们修复了在单击新建的批注外部时导致不清除文档中选定内容的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-199">We fixed an issue that caused the selection in the document to not be cleared when clicking outside a newly created comment.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-200">我们修复了如果文件名包含 DBCS 字符，则无法将邮件附件复制到除 Word 以外的应用程序这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-200">We fixed an issue where copying a mail attachment to an application other than Word would fail if the filename included DBCS characters.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-201">我们修复了将大声朗读与其他版本的 Windows 一起使用时导致意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-201">We fixed an issue that caused an expected close when using read aloud with other versions of Windows.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-202">修复了拼写和语法的画布上下文卡片显示图标按钮，但这些按钮没有工具提示这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-202">Fixed an issue where canvas contextual cards for spelling and grammar show icon buttons, but those buttons have no tooltips.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-203">我们修复了导致编辑器窗格主题和系统主题不匹配的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-203">We fixed an issue that was causing a mismatch between the Editor pane theme and the system theme.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-204">修复了编辑器窗格未打开这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-204">Fixed an issue where the Editor Pane doesn't open.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-205">修复了在编辑器中切换到“拼写检查”类别时相似度波形曲线未消失这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-205">Fixed an issue where similarity squiggles do not dissapear when switching to Spelling category in the Editor.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-206">我们修复了 Word 有时会在文本周围显示不应存在的边框的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-206">We fixed an issue where Word sometimes displayed a border around text that should not have been there.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-207">我们修复了特定字体旋转 90 度时字符间距增加这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-207">We fixed an issue where character spacing increases for specific fonts when rotating them 90 degrees.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-208">我们修复了在应用编辑限制的情况下运行宏时更新错误字段这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-208">We fixed an issue where the wrong field is getting updated when running a macro if editing restrictions are applied.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-209">我们修复了在与多个用户共同创作时批注回复有时丢失这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-209">We fixed an issue where comment replies were sometimes lost when coauthoring with multiple users.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-280">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-280">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-281">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-281">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-282">**Teams 网络研讨会与 Dynamics 365 Marketing 集成以支持潜在客户培养：** 借助此功能，网络研讨会组织者可以利用 D365 Marketing 推动与注册者的活动后互动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-282">**Teams Webinars integrate with Dynamics 365 Marketing to enable lead nurturing:** With this feature, webinar organizers can drive post event engagement with registrants by leveraging D365 Marketing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-283">与会者互动数据与 D365 Marketing 组织和启用的自动用户旅程同步</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-283">The attendee engagement data syncs with D365 Marketing org and enabled automated user journeys</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-284">**智能扬声器：** 智能扬声器是 Windows 上 Microsoft Teams 会议室的智能周边设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-284">**Intelligent speakers:** Intelligent speakers are intelligent peripherals for Microsoft Teams Rooms on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-285">与会者将为会议室中的与会者提供具有脚本的脚本，使与会者能够省下时间记笔记，并轻松跟进会议室中说了哪些内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-285">They will bring speaker attributed transcription for participants in the meeting room, enabling attendees to spend less time note-taking and easily follow along who said what in the room.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-286">**使 Teams 用户可以通过 Teams 客户端购买 Teams 应用：** Teams 用户现在能够从 Teams 商店购买 Teams 应用订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-286">**Enable Teams users to purchase Teams apps through Teams client:** Teams users have now the ability to purchase Teams app subscriptions from the Teams store.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-287">**使用团队模板创建 Teams：** 使用 Teams 中的模板，用户可以在创建新团队时从各种可自定义的模板中进行选择，以帮助他们快速入门。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-287">**Create Teams with Team Templates:** With Templates in Teams, users can choose from a variety of customizable templates when creating a new team, helping them get started quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-288">IT 管理员还可以为其组织创建自定义模板，从而使他们能够标准化团队结构，预安装相关应用并扩展最佳实践。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-288">IT Admins can also create custom templates for their organization, allowing them to standardize team structures, preinstall relevant apps, and scale best practices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-289">IT 管理员可以选择在 Teams 管理中心中向最终用户显示哪些团队模板，还可以通过在团队模板的网站选项卡中添加 URL 来预配置网站选项卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-289">IT Admins can choose which team templates to show to end users in Teams Admin Center, and also preconfigure website tabs by adding URLs to a website tab in a team template.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-290">**在 Teams 中的 PowerPoint Live 中使用激光笔和墨迹注释：** 我们推出了虚拟激光笔和注释，以便演示者可以吸引受众注意 PowerPoint 幻灯片组的某些部分，从而有效地共享内容并吸引受众。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-290">**Use laser pointer and ink annotations in PowerPoint Live in Teams:** We are introducing virtual laser pointer and annotations so presenters can effectively share content and engage their audience by drawing attention to certain sections of the PowerPoint deck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-291">就像在会议室使用物理激光笔一样，PowerPoint Live 可让你有效地指向不同位置，以便受众可以轻松地跟随幻灯片的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-291">Just as you would use a physical laser point in a room, PowerPoint Live allows you to effectively point at different places so the audience can easily follow along what’s on the slide.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-292">**通过 1P 团队模板实施 Power Automate 流程建议：** 为从 1P 团队模板创建的团队实施 Power Automate 流程模板</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-292">**Power Automate flow recommendations with 1P Team Templates:** Surface Power Automate flow templates for teams created from 1P team templates</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-319">**将布局引入 Teams 会议：** 现在，你可以叠加在内容上，获得更身临其境的演示和使用体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-319">**Introducing layouts to Teams meetings:** Now you can appear overlaid ontop of content for a more immersive presentation and consumption experience</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-320">**禁用特定与会者的照相机：** 会议组织者和演示者可以禁用 Teams 会议中特定与会者的照相机，以确保他们不会在会议中共享视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-320">**Disable Camera for Specific Attendees:** Meeting Organizers and Presenters can disable the cameras of specific Attendees in a Teams Meeting to make sure they don't share video in the meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-321">**禁用所有与会者的照相机：** 会议组织者和演示者可以禁用 Teams 会议中所有与会者的照相机，以确保他们不会在会议中共享视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-321">**Disable Camera for All Attendees:** Meeting Organizers and Presenters can disable the cameras of all Attendees in a Teams Meeting to make sure they don't share video in the meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-322">**匿名用户可以演示：** 托管 Teams 实时事件时，添加了匿名用户加入实时事件的能力，以便他们可以在事件期间进行演示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-322">**Anonymous users can present:** When hosting a Teams live event, we added the ability for an anonymous users to join a Live Event and so that they can also present during the event.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-323">**在 Teams 中以编程方式管理标签 - Microsoft Teams 标记 API 现已提供公共预览版：** 此组 API 可用于以编程方式在团队中分配用户标记，以便更快、更轻松地创建和维护标记。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-323">**Manage tags in Teams programmatically - Microsoft Teams Tags APIs are now in public preview:** This set of APIs can be used to programmatically assign users tags in a team, making tag creation and maintenance faster and easier.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-324">通过使用 Teams 中的标记，用户可快速联系一组人员，而无需 @mention 或键入所有人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-324">Tags in Teams let users quickly reach a group of people without having to @mention or type out everyone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-325">有关团队中标签详细信息，请参阅《在 Teams 使用标签》。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-325">For more information on tag in teams, see Using tags in Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-326">使用这些新的 API，开发人员现在可以在团队中创建标记，并在团队更新 tagsDelete 标记中向 usersGet 分配标记列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-326">Using these new APIs, developers can nowCreate tags in a team and assign usersGet a list of tags in a team Update tagsDelete tags</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-327">**从 PowerPoint 向 Teams 演示：** 通过 PowerPoint Live 直接从 PowerPoint 应用直向 Teams 会议演示幻灯片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-327">**Present from PowerPoint to Teams:** Present your slides directly from the PowerPoint app to a Teams meeting via PowerPoint Live.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-339">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-339">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-340">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-340">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-341">**在会议中同时聚焦多个用户：** 组织者和演示者现在可以在会议期间同时聚焦多个参与者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-341">**Spotlight multiple users at the same time in a meeting:** Organizers and presenters can now spotlight multiple participants simultaneously during meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-342">会议阶段将为会议中的每个人显示这些聚焦参与者及其视频或头像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-342">The meeting stage will show these spotlighted participants, with their videos or avatars, to everyone in the meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-343">**从 PowerPoint 演示到 Teams：** 通过 PowerPoint Live 将幻灯片从 PowerPoint 应用直接演示到 Teams 会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-343">**Present from PowerPoint to Teams:** Present your slides directly from the PowerPoint app to a Teams meeting via PowerPoint Live.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-344">**新增的标记管理体验和其他增强功能：Teams** 标签允许用户快速联系一组人员，而无需@mention或键入所有人。管理标记体验现更成为一个选项卡。标签现在还包括说明字段，以便向标记添加更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-344">**New manage tag experience and other enhancements:** Tags in Teams let users quickly reach a group of people without having to @mention or type out everyone.The manage tags experience is now a Tab. Tags also now have a description field so that you can add more details to a tag.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-345">新的"标记"选项卡将成为标记通知的登录页面，还会搜索标记（即将推出）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-345">The new Tags Tab will be the landing page for tag notifications and search for tags, which is also coming soon.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-346">**智能扬声器：** 智能扬声器是 Windows 上 Microsoft Teams 会议室的智能周边设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-346">**Intelligent Speakers:** Intelligent speakers are intelligent peripherals for Microsoft Teams Rooms on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-347">与会者将为会议室中的与会者提供具有脚本的脚本，使与会者能够省下时间记笔记，并轻松跟进会议室中说了哪些内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-347">They will bring speaker attributed transcription for participants in the meeting room, enabling attendees to spend less time note-taking and easily follow along who said what in the room.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-348">**将默认为本机通知，将新用户从团队紫色更改为本机通知：** 本机通知提供许多好处，例如支持操作中心、可访问性、对焦点辅助模式的支持。例如，目前 Microsoft Teams 中新用户的默认通知样式为"Teams 紫色"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-348">**Changing default to native notification from teams purple for new users:** Native Notifications provide a host of benefits like support for action center, accessibility, support for focus assist mode e.t.c.Currently the default notification style for a new user in Microsoft teams is Teams Purple.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-349">通过此更改，新用户的默认通知将更改为本机通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-349">With this change the default for new user will change to Native Notification.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-354">修复了在 64 位 Windows 使用 32 位 Office 时导致 Excel 意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-354">We fixed an issue that caused Excel to close unexpectedly when using 32 bit Office on 64 bit Windows.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-355">已修复了在"批注"窗格中移动批注时导致 Excel 意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-355">We fixed an issue that caused Excel to close unexpectedly when moving through comments in the Comments pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-356">解决了 Excel 无法加载某些自动化加载项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-356">Fixed an issue where some automation add-ins for Excel unable to load.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-357">我们修复了导致讲述人在 "页面设置" 对话框的 "页眉/页脚" 选项卡上错误地读取两个按钮属性的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-357">We fixed an issue that caused Narrator to incorrectly read the properties of two buttons on the Header/Footer tab in the Page Setup dialog box.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-358">修复了在运行更新链接时导致其他 Office 应用程序中链接的一些工作簿关闭而不保存更改的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-358">We fixed an issue that caused some workbooks linked in other Office applications to close without saving changes when running Update Link.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-359">解决了某些用户无法使用分析工具库加载项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-359">Fixed an issue where the Analysis ToolPak add-in did not work for some users.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-360">我们修复了某些文件在“受保护的视图”中偶尔会无法打开的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-360">We fixed an issue where some files would occasionally fail to open in Protected View</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-361">已修复使用加载项时导致某些语言的日期格式显示错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-361">We fixed an issue that caused date formatting to be displayed incorrectly in some languages when using add-ins.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-362">我们修复了导致某些用户的状态栏不显示“就绪”状态的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-362">We fixed an issue that caused the status bar to not indicate a Ready state for some users.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-363">我们做了一项更改，使名称管理器能够打开包含大量隐藏名称的书籍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-363">We made a change to enable the Name Manager to open on books with a large number of hidden names.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-p116">已修复相关问题来支持后向兼容性，以兼容老版本 Excel。由于自 Office 2007 以来在 Excel 中增加了 IFERROR 和 XLOOKUP 等功能，该问题可能导致在较新版本的 Excel 中保存的文件无法在较旧版本的 Excel 中正常加载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-p116">We fixed an issue to support backward compatibility with older versions of Excel. The issue may cause a file that is saved in a more recent version of Excel failed to load properly in older versions of Excel due to  functions such as IFERROR and XLOOKUP added to Excel since Office 2007.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-366">已修复在某些情况下将"选择性粘贴"与格式使用时可能会导致 Excel 意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-366">We fixed an issue which could cause Excel to close unexpectedly when using Paste Special with formats in certain situations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-373">我们解决了一个问题，即在Outlook中以从右到左的语言编写邮件时，将禁用包括数字的超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-373">We fixed an issue where hyperlinks including digits would be disable when composing a message in Outlook in a right-to-left language.</span></span>

### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-449">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-449">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-450">此更改修复了在某些情况下，运行 SQL Server 通过查询可能会导致错误消息表明存在"光标状态无效"的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-450">This change fixes an issue where in some cases running a SQL Server pass through query could result in an error message indicating that there was an "invalid cursor state".</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-453">修复了一个问题，阻止在受保护的工作表上粘贴为公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-453">We fixed a problem that was preventing the ability to paste as formulas on a protected sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-454">我们修复了如果文件保存为 PDF 文档，使用 HYPERLINK 功能创建的超链接将无法工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-454">We fixed an issue in which hyperlinks created using the HYPERLINK function would not work if the file was saved as a PDF document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-455">我们修复了一个问题，即隐式运算符 (@) 符号会添加到引用了空范围的公式中，且可能得出不正确的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-455">We fixed an issue where an implicit operator (@) symbol would be added to the formula with a reference to an empty range and potentially give the incorrect result.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-563">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-563">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-564">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-564">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-565">**对敏感加密文档自动保存和共同** ：不要为了安全而降低工作效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-565">**AutoSave and coauthoring on sensitive encrypted documents:** Don't trade off productivity for security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-566">使用 Microsoft 信息保护，现在像未加密文档一样，使用敏感度标签加密的文档可自动保存和他人共同创作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-566">With Microsoft Information Protection, documents that are encrypted with sensitivity labels can now be AutoSaved and co-authored with others in real time just like unencrypted documents can.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-567">需要租户选择加入（详细信息： https://aka.ms/mipcoauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-567">Requires tenant opt-in (more info: https://aka.ms/mipcoauth).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-575">**外出状态** 设置信息让他人知道你不在工作或正在休假，因此他们发聊天消息给你的时候你无法回复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-575">**Out of Office status** Set up a message to let others know you're not working or on vacation so you're not available to reply when they send a chat message to you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-576">你的外出状态也会和Outlook 日历中的自动答复同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-576">Your Out of Office status will also sync with Automatic Replies in your Outlook calendar.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-587">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-587">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-588">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-588">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-589">我们修复了删除外部驱动器时可能导致应用意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-589">We fixed an issue that could lead to an unexpected app close when removing an external drive.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-590">我们修复了外部应用程序请求辅助功能界面时，在其释放引用之前阻止我们关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-590">We fixed an issue when an external application requests an accessibility interface, it will prevent us from shutting down until they release their reference.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-591">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-591">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-592">我们修复了删除外部驱动器时可能导致应用意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-592">We fixed an issue that could lead to an unexpected app close when removing an external drive.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-593">解决了由于无法检索图像而尝试显示"数据类型"卡时 Excel 有时会意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-593">Fixed an issue where Excel would sometimes close unexpectedly when trying to show the Data Types card due to a not being able to retrieve an image.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-594">更正了使用乘法或日文字体除号时字体会意外更改的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-594">Corrected an issue where the font would change unexpectedly when using a multiplication or divide sign with a Japanese font.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-595">现在，如果支持该字符，我们将继续使用同一字体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-595">We now continue to use the same font if it supports the character.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-596">我们修复了一个阻止用户将 Excel 工作簿导出为 PDF 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-596">We fixed an issue that prevented users from exporting an Excel workbook to PDF.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-597">我们修复了使用“粘贴链接图片”选项时导致图像小于预期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-597">We fixed an issue which caused images to be smaller than expected when using the Paste Linked Picture option.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-598">我们修复了共同创作时复制工作表可能会丢失某些格式设置的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-598">We fixed an issue where some formatting could be lost when copying a sheet while coauthoring.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-599">我们修复了打开工作簿时意外显示某些笔记的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-599">We fixed an issue where some notes were unexpectedly shown when opening a workbook.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-600">我们修复了保存为 .xls 或 .xlt 格式时导致某些数据透视表格式设置损坏工作簿的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-600">We fixed an issue that caused some PivotTable formatting to corrupt the workbook when saving to the .xls or .xlt format.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-601">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-601">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-602">我们修复了删除外部驱动器时可能导致应用意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-602">We fixed an issue that could lead to an unexpected app close when removing an external drive.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-603">修复并解决了导致用户在创建新组后看到重复日历组的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-603">We fixed and issue that caused users to see duplicate calendar groups appearing after creating a new group.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-604">修复了导致“共享日历”改进用户无法将日历的颜色设置为黄色或棕色的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-604">We fixed an issue that caused users of the Shared Calendar improvements to be unable to set a calendar's color to yellow or brown.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-605">我们修复了导致用户看到新添加的日历直到 Outlook 重新启动之后才会显示在导航窗格中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-605">We fixed a problem that caused users to see newly added calendars fail to appear in the navigation pane until after Outlook had been restarted.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-606">我们修复了导出到 CSV 时导致非 ASCII 字符导出错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-606">We fixed an issue that caused non-ASCII characters to export incorrectly when exporting to CSV.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-607">我们修复了导致某些人员无法访问与辅助邮件账户相关联的签名的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-607">We fixed an issue that caused some people to be unable to access signatures associated with secondary mail accounts.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-608">我们修复了导致云设置功能用户在新设备上配置 Outlook 后会看到默认设置覆盖自定义设置的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-608">We fixed an issue that caused users of the Cloud Settings feature to see customized settings overridden by default setting after configuring Outlook on a new device.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-609">修复了导致用户看到包含 unicode 内容的签名受损的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-609">We fixed an issue that caused users to see signatures containing unicode content to get damaged.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-610">修复了导致内联翻译用户无法提交反馈的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-610">We fixed an issue that caused users of inline translation to be unable to submit feedback.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-611">我们已修复删除 DRM 保护时导致用户看到附件重复的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-611">We fixed an issue that caused users to see attachments getting duplicated when removing DRM protection.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-612">已修复了一个问题，即导致用户在撰写邮件时无法使用"检查姓名"来查找联系人组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-612">We fixed an issue that caused users to be unable to look up a contact group with Check Names  when composing mail.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-631">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-631">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-632">修复了这样一个问题，即如果用户未登录到可以访问 MIP 保护标签的标识，则使用 Microsoft 信息保护 （MIP） 标签打开的文件可能会无限期挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-632">We fixed an issue where opening a file protected with a Microsoft Information Protection (MIP) label can hang indefinitely if the user is not signed in to an identity that has access to the MIP protected label.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-633">用户被强制取消打开以显示登录提示，且该打开仅在这之后成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-633">The user is forced to cancel the open to show the sign-in prompt, and the open only succeeds after that point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-634">通过允许打开/下载期间显示登录提示来修复此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-634">Fixing this issue by allowing the sign-in prompt to be shown during open/download.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-635">我们修复了删除外部驱动器时可能导致应用意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-635">We fixed an issue that could lead to an unexpected app close when removing an external drive.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-636">修复了新"Word 批注"使用"听写"时的问题，批注卡中的"听写"按钮现在可正确开启和关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-636">We fixed an issue when using Dictation in the new Word Commenting, the Dictation button in the Comment card now correctly toggles on and off.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-637">共同创作文档时，活动草稿在批注顺序更改时没有清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-637">When coauthoring a document, active draft is not cleared when comment order changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-638">修复了用户口述录入文档时，字词间没有插入空格的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-638">Fixed an issue where there was no space being inserted between words when users dictated into their document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-639">修复了与包含滚动或缩放动画的滚动层有关的渲染管道中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-639">Fixes an issue in the rendering pipeline related to scrolling layers that contain scroll or zoom animations.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-640">我们修复了应用于图标和具有 3D 效果的 SVG 图形的颜色问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-640">Fixes an issue with colors applied to icons and SVG graphics with 3D effects.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-641">我们修复了自动保存中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-641">We fixed an issue in AutoSave.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-642">我们修复了脚注中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-642">We fixed an issue in footnote.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-841">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-841">Feature updates</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-843">**同时取消隐藏多张工作表：** 不再需要一次取消隐藏一个工作表，可以一次取消隐藏多个隐藏工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-843">**Unhide many sheets at the same time:** No need to unhide one sheet at a time anymore -- unhide multiple hidden sheets at once.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-844">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-844">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/69f2701a-21f5-4186-87d7-341a8cf53344)

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-845">**改进了条件格式对话框：** 条件格式对话框现在可以调整大小，现在只需单击一下即可复制规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-845">**Improved Conditional Formatting dialogs:** Conditional Formatting dialogs are now resizable, and now you can duplicate the rule with a single click.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-846">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-846">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/fed60dfa-1d3f-4e13-9ecb-f1951ff89d7f)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-849">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-849">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-850">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-850">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-851">修复了以下问题：Excel 错误地显示新版本文件可用的消息栏，并强制用户将更改保存在工作簿副本中或放弃更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-851">Fixed an issue where Excel would incorrectly show a message bar that a new version of the file is available and force the user to save their changes in a copy of the workbook or discard their changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-852">修复了 Selection.Parent.Copy 调用后切换分隔符的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-852">Fixed an issue with switching separators after a Selection.Parent.Copy call.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-853">将格式样式应用于数据透视表时，会提升性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-853">Made a performance improvement when applying formatting styles to pivot tables.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-854">修复了当打开包含 Excel 4.0 宏的 Excel 加载项文件时，Excel 可能会禁用宏而不提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-854">Fixed an issue where Excel may leave macros disabled without prompting when opening an Excel Add-in file containing Excel 4.0 Macros.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-855">更新以便在从 Excel 复制图表并粘贴到 Word 中时保留小数和千位分隔符设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-855">Update so that decimal and thousands separators settings carryover when copying a chart from Excel and pasting into Word</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-856">修正了当打开具有无效文件属性（创建时间、修改时间等）的 UNC 文件时，Excel 会意外关闭的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-856">Fixed an issue where Excel would close unexpectedly when opening UNC files that have invalid file attributes (creation time, modified time, etc.)</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-857">解决了使用 STOCKHISTORY 函数时可能会导致 "资源不足" 警报的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-857">Fixed an issue which could cause an "out of resources" alert when using the STOCKHISTORY function.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-858">已向 PQ dll 列表添加 FuzzyClustering dll。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-858">Added a FuzzyClustering dll to PQ dlls list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-859">此更改解决了与更改 SVG 图像的轮廓颜色有关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-859">This change addresses an issue related to changing outline colors of SVG images.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-860">我们已修复 PowerPoint 中的嵌入 Excel 区域预览显示错误大小的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-860">We have fixed an issue where Preview of embedded Excel range in PowerPoint shows incorrect size.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-919">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-919">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-920">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-920">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-921">**将有关敏感度标签的​​审核数据发送给 M365 管理员：** 用户在文档和电子邮件上应用、更改或删除敏感度标签时，Office 会将审核数据发送到 M365 审核后端，供管理员查看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-921">**Send audit data about sensitivity labeling to M365 administrators:** When users apply, change, or remove sensitivity labels on their documents and emails, Office will send up audit data to the M365 audit backend for administrators to see.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-922">这是一项静默功能（无 UI ），可让管理员受益。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-922">This is a silent functionality (no UI) for administrator benefit.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-959">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-959">Feature updates</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-960">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-960">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-961">**现在 Teams 支持 Windows 本机通知：** 用户现在可以通过 Teams 内置横幅或 Windows 本机横幅选择首选的通知传递方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-961">**Windows Native Notification are now Supported on Teams:** Users can now select their preferred means of notification delivery, either through Teams built-in banners or the Windows native banners.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-962">**Citrix 和 VMWare VDI 中的 Teams 会议 2x2 库视图：** 当 Teams 客户端处于 VDI 优化模式时，通过 VDI 上的 Teams 2x2 库视图功能，可以在 Citrix 和 VMWare 的 VDI 客户端上的 2x2 库视图中查看最多四个与会者视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-962">**Teams Meetings 2x2 Gallery View in Citrix and VMWare VDI:** Teams on VDI 2x2 Gallery View feature will enable to view up to four attendees videos in 2x2 Gallery View on VDI clients from Citrix, VMWare when Teams client in VDI optimized mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-963">**会议反应：** 会议反应是在会议中进行交互的新方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-963">**Meeting Reactions:**  Meeting reactions are a new way to interact in meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-964">参与者可以发送反应，这些反应将以流的形式显示在共享内容以及发送响应的个人上（如果它们在会议阶段显示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-964">Participants can send reactions which are shown as a stream on content that is being shared, and on the individual who sent the reaction if they're displayed on the meeting stage.</span></span> 


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-965">**Web 会议的同聚一堂模式和大型画廊模式** 大型画廊模式允许你一次观看多达 49 个其他用户的视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-965">**Together Mode and Large Gallery for Web Meetings** Large Gallery enables you to see the videos of up to 49 other people at once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-966">如果至少有 10 个人打开了相机，则此选项可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-966">This option is available when at least ten people have their cameras turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-967">同聚一堂模式可让你感觉自己与会议中的每个人处于同一个共享空间内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-967">Together mode lets you feel like you're in the same shared space with everyone in the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-968">当会议中至少有 5 个人时，同聚一堂模式可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-968">Together mode is available when there are at least five people in the meeting.</span></span> 


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-969">**呼叫合并** 呼叫合并允许用户将他们发出的新呼叫或新的来电合并到其一对一或群组呼叫中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-969">**Call Merge** Call Merge allows users to merge a new call they place, or a new incoming call, into their 1-1 or group call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-970">这适用于 Teams VOIP 呼叫和 PSTN 呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-970">This applies to Teams VOIP calls and PSTN calls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-980">我们已修复了从 OneDrive 本地同步文件夹插入文件时，插入对象命令不显示正确图标的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-980">We fixed an issue where the Insert Object command does not show the correct icon when inserting a file from OneDrive local sync folder.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-984">修复警报发生时与帮助文章断开的超链接，以防“自动保存”被禁用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-984">Fixed a broken hyperlink to a help article in an alert in case Autosave becomes disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-986">此更改解决了在公式中正确显示字体的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-986">This change addresses an issue with properly displaying fonts within equations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1001">我们已修复 Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 在使用传统视频格式（MPG-1、Mpeg-2）时崩溃的 VBA 问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1001">We fixed a VBA issue where Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 crashing with legacy video formats (MPG-1,Mpeg-2).</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1002">我们已修复以下问题：当有关 coauthor 的详细信息可用时，未知共同作者的状态指示器不会完全刷新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1002">We fixed an issue where an unknown coauthor's presence indicator does not get completely refreshed when more information about the coauthor is available.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1003">已固定开启标尺调整幻灯片视图大小时取消引用的 null 指针。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1003">Fixed a null pointer being dereferenced when slide view is resized with ruler turned on.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1004">已修复一些损坏的 PowerPoint 文件无法正常打开的问题，即使在执行文档修复操作后也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1004">Fixed an issue where some corrupt PowerPoint files were not opening correctly, even after a document repair operation.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1005">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1005">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1006">我们已修复用户在打开据推测已存储了更新信息的项目时，却无法找到所需更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1006">We fixed an issue where users open projects which have supposedly been saved with updated information, but find the updates are is missing.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1007">我们已修复如果交付项所关联的 SharePoint 站点不再存在，则无法删除这些交付结果的依赖关系的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1007">We fixed an issue where you couldn't delete dependencies on the deliverables if the SharePoint site the deliverable was associated with no longer existed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1008">已修复打开资源较多的项目耗时较长的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1008">Fixed an issue where opening a project with a lot of resources was taking a long time.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1009">已修复用户可能会看到多个与任务关联的未分配工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1009">Fixed an issue where users may see multiple unassigned assignments associated with a task.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1010">已修复大型项目中输入任务名称非常缓慢的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1010">Fixed an issue where in large projects it can be very slow to enter a task name.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1011">已修复项目文件加载到特定部分出现错误，导致可能打开特定项目的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1011">Fixed an issue where specific projects could be opened if there was an issue with the project file in a specific part of load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1019">我们已修复截断长超链接的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1019">We fixed an issue where long hyperlinks were getting truncated.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1098">修复了以下问题：当触发 MTR 计算和组策略对象更新进程（例如，通过远程组策略刷新）时，Excel 意外终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1098">We fixed an issue where Excel terminated unexpectedly when the process of MTR calc and Group Policy Object update (e.g. via Remote Group Policy Refresh) was triggered.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1102">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1102">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1103">修复了导致 Outlook 在添加或保存附件时偶尔停止工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1103">Addressed an issue which caused Outlook to stop working sporadically when adding or saving attachments.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-p159">已修复在快速打印图像附件时，产生错误提示：“Windows 无法找到此图片，请检查位置，然后重试”的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-p159">We fixed an issue where quick print for image attachments resulted in error, "Windows can't find this picture. Check the location, and then try again".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1106">修复了某些用户的 Outlook 会以脱机状态启动，需要他们手动选择联机工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1106">We fixed an issue that caused some users to see Outlook start in an Offline state until they manually chose to work online.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1107">修复了以下问题：当粘贴从会议位置复制的 URL 到其他地方（如浏览器）时，URL 的末尾包含分号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1107">We fixed an issue when pasting a URL copied from meeting location to somewhere else (such as a browser), the URL contains a semicolon at the end.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1108">修复了以下问题：用户无法在基本身份验证中删除 Microsoft 365 组的日历中的约会。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1108">We fixed an issue where users were unable to delete appointments in Calendar of Microsoft 365 Groups in Basic Auth.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1109">修复了加载昵称缓存时启动 Outlook 失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1109">We fixed an issue where starting Outlook failed while loading nickname cache.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1110">修复了以下问题：邮箱所有者无法管理自己日历的共享权限，因为该选项呈灰显。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1110">We fixed an issue where a mailbox owner wasn't able to manage Shared permission for their own Calendar as the option was greyed out.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1111">修复了 Outlook 无法使用受限权限创建邮件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1111">We fixed an issue where Outlook was not able to create a message with restricted permission.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1112">修复了将电子邮件模板另存为 .OFT 会将中文字符更改为问号的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1112">We fixed an issue where saving email templates as .OFT changed Chinese characters to question marks.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1113">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1113">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1114">我们解决了缩放显示区域导致缩放选择框和鼠标指针之间的差距的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1114">We fixed an issue where zooming in and out from the presentation area resulted in a gap between the zoomed selection marquee and the mouse pointer.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1115">修复了图片旁边的内容占位符图标没有工具提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1115">We fixed an issue where in content placeholder icon next to Pictures didn't have a tooltip.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1116">修复了由 pptsx 文件显示的幻灯片保护视图允许对受 IRM 保护的文件进行屏幕截图的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1116">We have fixed an issue where Protected view of slide show, shown by pptsx file, allows screen capture of IRM protected document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1117">修复了关闭设计窗格时，网格线在幻灯片上发生偏移的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1117">We fixed an issue where grid lines were getting shifted from slides when closing design pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1118">修复了以下问题：当复制幻灯片到辅助监视器，幻灯片可能隐藏在其他窗口后面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1118">We fixed an issue when duplicating slideshow to secondary monitor, the slideshow may hide behind other window.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1119">修复了以下问题：幻灯片中的滚动条在停止屏幕录制并打开选择窗格后开始自行调整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1119">We fixed an issue where the scroll bar in the slide starts adjusting itself after stopping screen recording with selection pane opened.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1120">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1120">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1121">修复了以下问题：如果在“任务窗体”类型视图中更改了滞后，ProjectBeforeTaskChagne 事件中的 NewVal 没有正确的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1121">Fixed an issue where the NewVal in the ProjectBeforeTaskChagne event doesn't have the correct value if a lag is changed within a Task Form type view.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1122">修复了当以某种方式指定资源分布时，项目可能在打开文件时意外终止的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1122">Fixed an issue where Project may terminate unexpectedly on opening files where resource contours were specified in a certain manner.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1123">修复了以下问题：将项目从 PWA 保存到本地 mpp 文件时，用户实际上未更改的数据将触发 ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1123">Fixed an issue where when you save a project from PWA to a local mpp file, the ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent fires for data that wasn't actually changed by the user.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1124">修复了以下问题：资源预订按名称而不是按 GUID 搜索资源，如果存在多个具有相同名称的资源，则会导致问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1124">Fixed an issue where resource engagements searched for a resource by name instead of GUID which would cause issues if there were multiple resources with the same name.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1125">修复了以下问题：如果你在项目网站中有任务列表并对任务列表进行了分组，将无法快速编辑任务列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1125">Fixed an issue where if you have a task list in a project site and group the task list, you will not be able to quick edit the task list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1126">修复了以下问题：如果通过 CSOM 更新企业资源，可能会丢失资源最大单位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1126">Fixed an issue where if you update an enterprise resource via CSOM, resource max units may be lost.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1132">修复了将 Excel 工作簿插入 Word 文档时，Word 似乎会挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1132">We fixed an issue where Word appears to hang when inserting an Excel workbook into a Word document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1236">修复了加载查询/关系窗口时，未正确设置滚动条位置的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1236">We fixed an issue where scrollbar position was not set correctly when loading query/relationship window saved while scrolled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1237">修复了“添加表格”任务窗格未正确显示包含“&”的名称的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1237">We fixed an issue where Add Table Task Pane was not displaying names containing '&' correctly.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1238">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1238">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1239">修复了多级分类手动间隔未在图表中运行的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1239">We fixed an issue where multi-level category manual interval was not working in charts.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1240">修复了二维地图图表在使用 VBA 设置系列的最大值、中间值和最小值的颜色时，无法正常工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1240">Fixed an issue with 2D Map Charts where using VBA to set the colors for the max, mid, and min values for a series was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1241">修复了可能导致“Excel 在尝试计算一个或多个公式时用尽资源”错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1241">Fixed an issue which could cause an error that "Excel ran out of resources while attempting to calculate one or more formulas".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1242">修复了将 Office 语言设置为西班牙语时出现的问题，在有问题的情况下，数据验证列表可能不会显示列表中的所有项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1242">Fixed an issue when the Office language was set to Spanish, in which data validation lists may not show all the items in the list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1243">修复了以下问题：在启用了“分页预览”的情况下，在具有大量数据的工作表之间切换时，可能会出现明显的延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1243">Fixed an issue where there could be a noticeable delay when switching between worksheets with large amounts of data when 'Page Break Preview' was enabled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1244">修复了向用于数据验证的表格添加内容时，未更新工作簿中所有工作表的选项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1244">We fixed an issue where adding to a table used for Data Validation did not update options for all sheets in the workbook.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1245">修复了在刷新 OLAP 数据透视表时可能会导致挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1245">We fixed an issue which could cause a hang when refreshing OLAP PivotTables.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1246">修复了通过公式栏输入公式时，ChartSheet 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1246">Fixed an issue where ChartSheet crashed in some cases when a formula is entered through formula bar.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1247">修复了当设备连接丢失（例如远程会话连接/断开或显示器更改）后，Excel 编辑栏不会完全呈现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1247">We fixed an issue where the Excel formula bar would not render completely after connection to a device was lost, such as a remote session connect/disconnect or a monitor change.</span></span>


### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1248">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1248">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1250">修复了将鼠标悬停在笔记本颜色选择器中的绿色颜色上时，弹出窗口显示“红色粉笔”的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1250">We fixed an issue when you hover over green color in notebook color selector, the pop up reads "red chalk".</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1252">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1252">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1253">解决了以下问题：当主题为空白时，自动生成的电子邮件将发送空白正文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1253">Addresses an issue that caused automatically generated emails to be sent with a blank body when the subject is blank.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1254">修复了为文件夹缓存错误的文件夹 GUID 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1254">We fixed an issue where the wrong folder guid is cached for folders.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1255">当用户将电子邮件地址和显示名称复制并粘贴到收件人字段时，该电子邮件地址始终不会被正确分析，并导致出现有关电子邮件地址无效的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1255">When a user copy-and-pastes an email address into the recipient field with the display name, the email address wasn't always parsed correctly and caused a warning about an invalid email address to appear.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1256">已对其进行修复，以便正确分析名称和电子邮件地址，所以不会再显示该警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1256">It's been fixed so the name and email address are parsed correctly so the warning is no longer shown.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1257">修复了联机共享文件夹未返回父文件夹名称的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1257">We fixed an issue where online shared folders did not return parent folder name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1258">并非返回失败，而是返回一个空路径，该路径错误地转到主帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1258">Intsead of failing, it returned an empty path which incorrectly went to the primary account.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1259">修复了“另存为”选项不可用于经典附件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1259">We fixed an issue where the Save As option was not available for classic attachments.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1260">修复了替代策略时为用户提供自定义对齐文本方法的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1260">We fixed an issue to provide a user a way to customize justification text when overriding a policy.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1261">修复了从只读预览窗格中重新打开草稿后启用修订的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1261">We fixed an issue where track changes turned on after reopening draft from read-only preview pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1262">修复了在关闭重点收件箱并执行排序后隐藏电子邮件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1262">We fixed an issue with emails being hidden after turning Focused Inbox off and doing a sort.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1263">修复了导致 Outlook 为已启用云设置的用户创建第二个空签名的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1263">We fixed an issue that caused Outlook to create a second empty signature for people who had cloud settings enabled.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1269">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1269">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1270">修复了以下问题：如果尝试多次添加相同项目且 AttachToSources 设置为 False，ConsolidateProjects VBA 方法可能失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1270">Fixed an issue where the ConsolidateProjects VBA method may file if you try to add the same project multiple times and have AttachToSources set to false.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1271">修复了以下问题：如果你正在运行事件代码并尝试通过 “任务窗体”视图进行更改，单击“确定”按钮可能无法提交所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1271">Fixed an issue where if you have eventing code running and try to make changes through a Task Form view, clicking the OK button may not commit the changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1272">修复了以下问题：如果尝试多次添加相同项目且 AttachToSources 设置为 False，ConsolidateProjects VBA 方法可能失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1272">Fixed an issue where the ConsolidateProjects VBA method may file if you try to add the same project multiple times and have AttachToSources set to false.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1273">修复了以下问题：如果你有带公式的自定义字段且使用挣值，你可能会注意到切换视图和打开项目/任务详细信息时的性能延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1273">Fixed an issue where if you have custom fields with formulas and are using earned value, you may notice performance delays switching views and opening project/task details.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1274">修复了以下问题：如果将“分组依据”应用于“资源使用状况”或“工作表视图”，然后插入一列，Project 可能崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1274">Fixed an issue where Project may crash if you apply a group by to the Resource Usage or Sheet view and then insert a column.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1277">已修复当用户点击修订（插入/删除）时，将显示批注弹出窗口的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1277">Fixed an issue where a user tapping on a tracked change (insertion/deletion) would bring up a comment pop-out.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1278">我们已修复了在 Word 中删除批注标注的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1278">We fixed an issue with deleting comment callouts in Word.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1279">我们已修复了 Outlook 邮件设置为“不要转发”的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1279">We fixed an issue with Outlook with message set to Do not forward.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1280">我们已修复了保存 Word 文档（包含引文和公式）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1280">We fixed an issue with saving Word document that contains citation and equation.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1281">我们修复了“样式库”对话框的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1281">We fixed an issue with Style Gallery dialog.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1282">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1282">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-p173">当用户在办公室的喷墨打印机上打印任何文档/文件，并且打印机墨水不足时，即使喷墨打印机不需要碳粉，也会显示 "碳粉不足 "或 "无碳粉 "的信息。将信息更改为显示“碳粉/墨水不足”&“无碳粉/墨水”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-p173">When the user prints any document/file on inkjet printers from Office and printer's ink is low, "Toner Low" or "No Toner" message will show, even though inkjet printers don't have toners. Changing message to display "Toner/ink Low" & "No toner/ink".</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1392">如果用户键入了包含圆括号的公式名称，并通过 F1 调用了帮助，则特定于该公式的帮助主题将不会显示，我们已解决了这个问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1392">We fixed an issue where if a user typed a formula name including the parenthesis and invoked help via F1, the help topic specific to that formula would not be displayed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1394">修复了用户无法修改数据透视表筛选器的问题，因为它被设置为在 Analysis Services 数据库中已不存在的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1394">We fixed an issue where users could not modify a PivotTable filter because it was set to a value that was no longer present in an Analysis Services database.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1395">修复了与 XLAM 外接程序引用和命名区域相关的崩溃问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1395">Fixed a crash related to XLAM add-in references and named ranges.</span></span>

This was a legacy restriction that has been removed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1406">修复了从一个空联系人组向另一个联系人组发送会议请求时会导致崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1406">We fixed a condition where sending a meeting request from an empty contact group to another contact group would result in a crash.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1519">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1519">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1520">我们修复了以下问题：图表系列的顺序发生更改时，与序列保持一致的对应复选框未与序列一起重新排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1520">We fixed an issue where if the order of a chart series was changed, the corresponding checkbox aligned with the series was not reordered along with the series.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2fd4c-1521">当试图使用LET()函数保存包含公式的文件时，可能会出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2fd4c-1521">An error could occur when trying to save a file that contains a formula using the LET() function.</span></span>
